***uier.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:uier.html>uier</a> (98344)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">uider</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">ûder</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*ūdar</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*ūdarą</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">udder</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">udder</i>.

***uil.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:uil.html>uil</a> (10955)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">ule</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*ūwila</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*ūwala</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*ūla</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*uwwalǭ</i>, diminutive of <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*uwwǭ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">eagle-owl</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, of imitative origin or a variant of <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*ūfaz</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*ūfǭ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uil.html>uil</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uilen.html>uilen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uiltje.html>uiltje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:birds.html>birds</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> owl, bird of the order Strigiformes
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl">'s <a href = vnd.unilang:avonds.html>Avonds</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zitten.html>zitten</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>er</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:uilen.html>uilen</a></b> in <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:boom.html>boom</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bij.html>bij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:buren.html>buren</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">In the evening there are <b><a href = vnd.unilang:owls.html>owls</a></b> in the neighbours' tree.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">insects</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">noctuoid</span>, owl moth, owlet
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:veel.html>Veel</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:uilen.html>uilen</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:hebben.html>hebben</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:typerend.html>typerende</a> uilvlekken.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Many <b>owlet moths</b> have characteristic wing marks.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">insects<span class="ib-comma">,</span> dialectal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">butterfly</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">generic term</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:deze.html>Deze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kleurrijke.html>kleurrijke</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:uiltje.html>uiltjes</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:eten.html>eten</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nectar.html>nectar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:uitwerpselen.html>uitwerpselen</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">These colourful <b>butterflies</b> eat <a href = vnd.unilang:nectar.html>nectar</a> and excrement.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> idiot
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>Die</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:uil.html>uil</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:minerva.html>Minerva</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:spreidt.html>spreidt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zich.html>zich</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vleugel.html>vleugel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bij.html>bij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vallen.html>vallen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:avond.html>avond</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">That <b><a href = vnd.unilang:nutter.html>nutter</a></b> from the Oxford Union lies down to mount his grand <a href = vnd.unilang:piano.html>piano</a> when the night falls.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***uit.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>uit</a> (60)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">uut</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:ute.html>ute</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">ūt</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*ūt</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">út</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">out</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">aus</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">ud</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb_2">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>uit</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>out, from the inside to the outside</li>
<li>out, off <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to an extinguished or switched-off state</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vuur.html>vuur</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>uit</a></b>.</i>
<dl><dd>The fire <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b>out</b>.</dd></dl></dd>
<dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:televisie.html>televisie</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>uit</a></b>.</i>
<dl><dd>The television <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b>off</b>.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li><a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a>, finished, completely
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:spel.html>spel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>uit</a></b>.</i>
<dl><dd>The game <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a></b>.</dd></dl></dd>
<dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zij.html>Zij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:las.html>las</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:boek.html>boek</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:helemaal.html>helemaal</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>uit</a></b>.</i>

***uitdelen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:uitdelen.html>uitdelen</a> (8383)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>uit</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:delen.html>delen</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uitdelen.html>uitdelen</a></strong>
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:uitdrukken.html>uitdrukken</a> (12740)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">uutdrucken</i>, equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>uit</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">out</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:drukken.html>drukken</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to press</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. In the sense “to express” a calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">exprimere</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">ausdrücken</i>.

***uiteinde.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:uiteinde.html>uiteinde</a> (16936)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">uit-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:einde.html>einde</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uiteinde.html>uiteinde</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uiteinden.html>uiteinden</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl">uiteindes</b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uiteinde.html>uiteindje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>

***uitgaan.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:uitgaan.html>uitgaan</a> (3094)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">ûtegâen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">ūtgān</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>uit</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gaan.html>gaan</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uitgaan.html>uitgaan</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to go out <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to go to public <a href = vnd.unilang:places.html>places</a> for leisure</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to turn off, to shut down</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to expire, to break up (of a relationship)</li></ol>

***uitgang.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:uitgang.html>uitgang</a> (3570)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">ūtgang</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*ūtgang</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*ūtgangaz</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Ausgang</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">outgang</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uitgang.html>uitgang</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uitgangen.html>uitgangen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uitgang.html>uitgangetje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">exit</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">outgang</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">electronics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> output</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">linguistics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> ending, termination</li></ol>

***uitgave.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:uitgave.html>uitgave</a> (12659)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From the verb <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uitgeven.html>uitgeven</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to give out, to spend</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>uit</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gave.html>gave</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uitgave.html>uitgave</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uitgave.html>uitgaves</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uitgaven.html>uitgaven</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uitgave.html>uitgavetje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl">uitgaafje</b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>edition, e.g. of a publication</li>
<li>release, e.g. of an album</li>
<li>monetary expense</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>See the etymology of the main entry.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uitgave.html>uitgave</a></strong>
